SRD Status Check for R370 2026</h1></header><div class="entry-content single-content"><p>You can use the below <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/">SASSA Status Check</a> to find your R370 (previously R350) and other grants status within one click by providing your South African ID Number and Phone Number.</p><div class='code-block code-block-6' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div id="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><div class="wp-block-kadence-advancedbtn kb-buttons-wrap kb-btns28_e45998-c2"><a class="kb-button kt-button button kb-btn28_22f4d9-12 kt-btn-size-xlarge kt-btn-width-type-full kb-btn-global-fill kt-btn-has-text-true kt-btn-has-svg-false wp-block-kadence-singlebtn" href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><span class="kt-btn-inner-text"><mark style="background-color:rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)" class="has-inline-color has-theme-palette-3-color"><strong>Check Status</strong></mark></span></a></div><p class="has-text-align-center">Last updated: <strong>Monday 23 February 2026</strong></p><p><strong>Found an Issue?</strong> If you are facing any issue while checking your SASSA or SRD status, feel free to <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/contact-us/" data-type="page" data-id="66">contact us</a> and report it. For any issue related to your grant or other than our website, please <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-contact-details/" data-type="page" data-id="253">contact SASSA</a> directly.</p><p>Check the following steps to use SASSA Status Checker available on the official SASSA website which can be opened by clicking on the button given above,</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li>Enter your South African ID Number in the first box</li><li>Enter your Phone Number in the second box</li><li>Click on “submit”</li></ol><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>After clicking on “submit” button, your application status result will be shown.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Payment_Dates_for_2026-27">SASSA Payment Dates for 2026-27</span></h2><p>Payment dates for the payment cycle from April 2025 to March 2026 is given below.</p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full has-custom-border"><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2025-2026.webp"><img fetchpriority="high" decoding="async" width="1448" height="2048" src="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2025-2026.webp" alt="SASSA Payment Dates for 2025-2026" class="has-border-color has-theme-palette-2-border-color wp-image-726" style="border-width:2px" srcset="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/04/SASSA-Payment-Dates-for-2025-2026.webp 1448w, class="wp-element-caption">SASSA Payment Dates for 2026-27</figcaption></figure></div><div style="height:10px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div><p>Note: SASSA Payment Dates schedule for 2026-27 (April 2026 to March 2027) will be released officially by SASSA in March 2026.</p><p>Check more details about <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-payment-dates/" data-type="page" data-id="208">SASSA Payment Dates 2026/2027</a>.</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" data-align="center">Wednesday</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">9:00 AM to 5:00 PM</td></tr></tbody></table></figure><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SRD_Status_Meanings">SRD Status Meanings</span></h2><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>You will get the following possible outcome after checking your status on our website or the official one.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Application Complete:</strong> Your application has been received. Wait for SASSA to start the verification process.</li><li><strong><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-status-pending/" data-type="page" data-id="219">Pending</a>:</strong> Your application is being verified by SASSA. No action is required.</li><li><strong>Approved:</strong> Your grant is approved for the month shown. Payments are on the way.</li><li><strong><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-status-decline/" data-type="page" data-id="228">Declined</a>:</strong> Your application was rejected for a specific reason, which will be listed. You can <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-appeal/" data-type="page" data-id="245">appeal</a> this decision.</li><li><strong><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-reapplication/" data-type="page" data-id="168">Reapplication Pending</a>:</strong> You must submit a new application to be considered for a grant.</li><li><strong>Identity Verification Failed:</strong> Your ID or name on the application does not match Home Affairs records.<ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Action:</strong> Correct your details and re-apply, or lodge an appeal.</li></ul></li><li><strong>Referred to SASSA:</strong> Your application needs a manual review by a SASSA official.</li><li><strong><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-banking-details/" data-type="page" data-id="215">Bank Details Pending</a>:</strong> You have not provided your banking details.<ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Action:</strong> Submit or update them on the official SASSA website.</li></ul></li><li><strong><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-status-check-failed/" data-type="page" data-id="222">Failed</a>:</strong> Your payment could not be processed, likely due to incorrect bank details or a closed account.<ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Action:</strong> Correct your banking details on the official SASSA website.</li></ul></li><li><strong>Cancelled:</strong> Your grant was cancelled. If you did not do this, contact SASSA immediately.</li></ul><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Check_your_Status_Online">How to Check your Status Online</span></h2><p><strong>Note:</strong> Check the following video created by us to see how to check SASSA Status using our website <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/">sassacheckstatus.co.za</a>.</p><figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">
<iframe loading="lazy" title="SASSA Status Check | SASSA SRD R370 Status Check 2025" width="720" height="405" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/XeP2p6fppFQ?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin" allowfullscreen></iframe></div></figure><p>You can follow the steps given below to check your SASSA Status online if you are having issue with the above video.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Status_Check_online">SASSA Status Check online</span></h3><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Using_Official_Website">Using Official Website</span></h4><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>Using the official source to check your status is recommended if you are conscious about using government source only.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Open <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status</a></li><li>Enter your South African ID Number (13 digits)</li><li>Enter your Phone Number (10 digits)</li><li>Click on “submit”</li><li>It will show you the status of your application</li></ul><p>Note: Currently, this official page is not available on Google due to some unknown reason so you can visit this page directly by clicking on the above link.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_SRD_R370_Status_Check_by_SMS">SASSA SRD R370 Status Check by SMS</span></h3><p>You can always send a text message through any mobile phone. Messaging apps are available in every mobile phone whether is a keypad or android. You can follow the steps given below for SASSA SRD Status Check by SMS,</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Open Messages app on your mobile phone</li><li>Enter the text “SASSA (ID Number)”. Here the South African ID Number is your valid South African ID. For example, “SASSA 8608802039”</li><li>Send this Message to <strong>082 046 8553</strong></li><li>You will receive your SASSA Payment status in reply after a while</li></ul><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_SRD_Status_Check_by_WhatsApp">SASSA SRD Status Check by WhatsApp</span></h3><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>You can also access your SRD Status Check and SASSA Status Check for R350 Payment Dates via WhatsApp for free, by sending an sms to <a href="tel:+27820468553">082 054 0016</a>, if you have your <strong>Form Reference Number</strong>. Follow these steps:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Save the SASSA WhatsApp number <a href="tel:+27820540016">082 054 0016</a> to your phone contacts.</li><li>Open a chat with the SASSA number and type “Status”&nbsp;</li><li>Enter your form reference number as prompted</li><li>An automated response will provide your application status and details</li><li>You can type “SASSA” to get back to the main menu where you can apply for SRD Grant as well.</li></ul><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-full is-resized has-custom-border"><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/SASSA-Status-Check-WhatsApp-Number.webp"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="450" height="967" src="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/SASSA-Status-Check-WhatsApp-Number.webp" alt="SASSA Status Check WhatsApp Number" class="has-border-color has-theme-palette-2-border-color wp-image-1976" style="border-width:2px;width:300px;height:undefinedpx" srcset="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/SASSA-Status-Check-WhatsApp-Number.webp 450w, https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2025/08/SASSA-Status-Check-WhatsApp-Number-140x300.webp 140w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 450px) 100vw, 450px"></a><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">SASSA Status Check WhatsApp Number</figcaption></figure></div><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_SRD_Status_Check_by_USSD">SASSA SRD Status Check by USSD</span></h3><p>A USSD SASSA status check for SRD R370 can be done by dialing <strong><a href="tel:*120*69277#">*120*3210#</a></strong> or <strong><a href="tel:*120*69277#">*120*69277#</a></strong> on your cellphone to check your balance and grant status, then follow the prompts.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Status_Check_Appeal">SASSA Status Check Appeal</span></h2><p>If your SASSA SRD grant application was rejected, don’t worry. You can send <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-appeal-status-check/" data-type="page" data-id="318">SASSA Status Check appeal</a> online and ask SASSA to check your case again. This is called <strong>“<a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-status-reconsideration/" data-type="page" data-id="225">reconsideration</a>”</strong> You can also appeal if the <strong>Independent Tribunal for Social Assistance Appeals (ITSAA)</strong> rejected your appeal. You must do this <strong>within 90 days</strong>.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Send_an_SASSA_Appeal_Online">How to Send an SASSA Appeal Online</span></h3><ol class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Go to the official SASSA SRD website:</strong> <a class="" href="http://srd.sassa.gov.za" target="_blank" rel="noopener">http://srd.sassa.gov.za</a></li><li><strong>Click on “Appeal” button</strong> on the website homepage</li><li><strong>Enter your South African ID number (13 digits)</strong> and the <strong>phone number</strong> you used when applying</li><li><strong>SASSA will send you a PIN</strong> code through SMS</li><li><strong>Enter the PIN</strong> on the website to verify your number</li><li><strong>Select the month</strong> your application was rejected<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>You must send a <strong>separate appeal for each month</strong> you were declined</li></ul></li><li><strong>Upload important documents</strong>, like:<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Proof of where you live</li><li>Bank statements (last 6 months)</li></ul></li><li><strong>Write a short reason</strong> why you are appealing<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Example: “I lost my job. I have no other income.”</li></ul></li><li><strong>Click “Submit”</strong> to send your appeal to SASSA</li></ol><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Check_Your_Appeal_Status">How to Check Your Appeal Status</span></h3><ol class="wp-block-list"><li>Visit the <strong>SASSA Appeal Status Check page</strong><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals" target="_blank" rel="noopener">https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals</a></li></ul></li><li>Enter your <strong>ID number</strong> and the <strong>same phone number</strong> you used</li><li>SASSA will send an <strong>OTP code</strong> (One-Time PIN) to your phone</li><li>Enter the OTP code on the website</li><li>Your <strong>appeal status</strong> will show on the screen</li></ol><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Reinstate_Your_SASSA_SRD_R370_Grant">How to Reinstate Your SASSA SRD R370 Grant</span></h3><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>If you canceled your SRD grant before (for example, because you got a job), but now you need help again, you can <strong>reinstate</strong> it.</p><ol class="wp-block-list"><li>Go to the <strong>SASSA website</strong>: <a class="" href="http://srd.sassa.gov.za" target="_blank" rel="noopener">http://srd.sassa.gov.za</a></li><li>Enter your <strong>ID number</strong> and <strong>phone number</strong></li><li>Click “Send PIN” and enter the OTP code from SMS</li><li>Choose your <strong>reason for reinstating</strong>:<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>I don’t have a job anymore</li><li>I canceled by mistake</li></ul></li><li>Click “Confirm”</li></ol><p>SASSA will check your request in <strong>7 to 14 days</strong>. If approved, you will get a message.</p><div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column28_93438a-af"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><h4 class="wp-block-heading has--font-size"><span id="Important_Tips">Important Tips</span></h4><ol class="wp-block-list has-sm-12-font-size"><li>Always use the <strong>same ID number and phone number</strong> that you used during the application.</li><li>You can only <strong>appeal online</strong> once per month.</li><li>Make sure your <strong>documents are clear</strong> and easy to read.</li><li>You cannot appeal by email or SMS. Use the <strong>online method</strong> for faster results.</li></ol></div></div><p>Checking your SASSA status frequently gives you the details needed to proactively manage your grant application and resolve any issues without delay.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Change_Your_SASSA_Banking_Details"><strong>How to Change Your SASSA Banking Details</strong></span></h3><p>Follow these steps to <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-banking-details/" data-type="page" data-id="215">update your banking information</a> and ensure your payments are sent to the correct account.</p><ol start="1" class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Access the Website:</strong> Go to the official <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA SRD website</a>.</li><li><strong>Enter ID:</strong> Find the “Change Banking Details” section and enter your South African ID number.</li><li><strong>Receive SMS:</strong> You will receive a secure SMS link to your registered mobile number.</li><li><strong>Open the Link:</strong> Click the unique link from the SMS. It will take you to a secure portal.</li><li><strong>Enter Details:</strong> Follow the prompts to enter your new bank account information.<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>You can choose a bank account or a Postbank option.</li></ul></li><li><strong>Verify:</strong> After submitting, the new details will undergo a verification process.<ul class="wp-block-list"><li>This can take some time. Once verified, your grant payments will be sent to the new account.</li></ul></li></ol><p><em>Note: Your new bank account must be in your name as per the official SASSA records. SASSA cannot pay grants into a third-party account.</em></p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="What_SASSA_Banking_Details_Pending_Means"><strong>What ‘SASSA Banking Details Pending’ Means</strong></span></h3><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>A ‘Banking Details Pending’ status means SASSA has received your application but does not have a valid bank account to pay your grant into. This status is common for new applicants or those who have recently changed their banking details.</p><p><strong>What to Do:</strong></p><ol start="1" class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Submit Details:</strong> If you have not submitted your details, do so immediately using the steps above.</li><li><strong>Check for Errors:</strong> If you have already submitted details, there might be a small error (e.g., incorrect ID number, name mismatch with the bank account).</li><li><strong>Be Patient:</strong> The verification process can take time. Avoid re-submitting your details multiple times as this can cause delays. Wait a few days to a week for the status to change.</li></ol><p><em>A ‘Bank Details Pending’ status must be resolved before any approved payments can be made.</em></p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Awaiting_Identity_Verification"><strong>SASSA ‘Awaiting Identity Verification’</strong></span></h2><p>The South African Social Security Agency (SASSA) performs identity verification to confirm you are who you say you are. This process links your application details to your official record at the Department of Home Affairs (DHA). It’s an important step to prevent fraud and ensure only eligible citizens receive grants.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Why_Identity_Verification_Fails"><strong>Why Identity Verification Fails</strong></span></h3><p>An “Identity Verification Failed” status means the information you provided to SASSA does not match the records with the DHA.<sup></sup> This can happen for several reasons:</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Mismatched Personal Details:</strong> Your name, surname, or ID number on the application differs from what is on your official ID.</li><li><strong>Outdated Information:</strong> Your details with the DHA may be outdated due to a name change or other personal status change.</li><li><strong>ID Book vs. Smart Card:</strong> For some verification methods, having an old green ID book may cause issues with the system’s ability to get a clear image.</li><li><strong>Typos:</strong> Simple errors like a misspelled name or an incorrect digit in your ID number will cause a failure.</li></ul><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="How_to_Fix_a_Failed_Identity_Check"><strong>How to Fix a Failed Identity Check</strong></span></h3><p>If your status shows “Identity Verification Failed,” you must take action to get it resolved.<sup></sup> Failure to do so can result in your grant remaining suspended.<sup></sup></p><ol start="1" class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Check Your Details:</strong> First, confirm that the ID number and name you entered on your application are 100% correct.</li><li><strong>Lodge an Appeal:</strong> You must appeal a declined application to have your case reviewed. The appeal will be handled by the Independent Tribunal for Social Assistance Appeals (ITSAA). You can appeal against your application <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>. When you appeal, be prepared to submit documents that prove your identity and address the reason for the decline.</li><li><strong>Biometric Verification:</strong> In some cases, SASSA may require you to complete a biometric verification, which involves fingerprint or facial recognition checks. This is usually done at a SASSA office or a partner retail outlet and is required to unlock your account.</li><li><strong>Contact Home Affairs:</strong> If you have corrected your details and the verification still fails, your information may be incorrect at the DHA. You might need to visit a DHA office to confirm and correct your records.</li></ol><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Why_Your_SASSA_Money_Is_Not_In"><strong>Why Your SASSA Money Is Not In</strong></span></h3><p>It’s frustrating when you expect a payment and it doesn’t arrive. Here are the most common reasons for a delayed or missed SASSA grant payment, along with what you should do to fix it.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Payment_Has_Not_Been_Processed_Yet"><strong>Payment Has Not Been Processed Yet</strong></span></h4><p>SASSA payments are not all made on the same day. While the agency gives a payment week, payments are processed in batches. Your payment may simply be scheduled for a later day in that week.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Solution:</strong> <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Check your SASSA status</a> online. If it shows <strong>“Approved”</strong> for the current month and has a payment date, your money is on its way. Be patient and check your bank account again in a day or two.</li></ul><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Incorrect_or_Pending_Banking_Details"><strong>Incorrect or Pending Banking Details</strong></span></h4><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>This is a very frequent reason for failed payments. If your bank details are incorrect or have not been verified, SASSA cannot send the money. This includes having a closed account or using a third-party account that is not in your name.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Solution:</strong> Your SASSA status will show <strong>“Banking Details Pending”</strong> or <strong>“Failed.”</strong> Go to the official SASSA website to update or re-submit your correct bank details. Make sure the account is in your name and active.</li></ul><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="Failed_Identity_Verification"><strong>Failed Identity Verification</strong></span></h4><p>The South African Social Security Agency (SASSA) checks your ID number and personal details against the Home Affairs database. If there is a mismatch, your application and payments will be suspended to prevent fraud.</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Solution:</strong> Your status will show <strong>“Identity Verification Failed.”</strong> You must appeal this decision on the <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">official SASSA appeal website</a>. If you’ve changed your name or surname, confirm your details are updated with Home Affairs.</li></ul><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Has_Assessed_You_as_Ineligible"><strong>SASSA Has Assessed You as Ineligible</strong></span></h4><p>Eligibility for the SRD grant is assessed monthly. If your income or assets were flagged by the system, you will be found ineligible for that month.</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Solution:</strong> Your status will be <strong>“Declined”</strong> with a specific reason like “Alternative Income Source Identified.” You can appeal this decision if you believe the assessment is incorrect.</li></ul><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SRD_Alternative_Income_Source_Identified"><strong>SRD “Alternative Income Source Identified”</strong></span></h2><p>This is based on a <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-means-test/" data-type="post" data-id="974">means test</a>. It indicates that SASSA has detected an income stream that disqualifies you. The “alternative” part means it could be from a source other than a regular salary, such as:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>A private pension.</li><li>Business profits.</li><li>Other grants.</li><li>Maintenance payments.</li><li>Funds received from family members.</li></ul><p><strong>How it works:</strong> SASSA cross-references your ID number with various databases, including:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>SARS (South African Revenue Service):</strong> To check for formal employment income.</li><li><strong>UIF (Unemployment Insurance Fund):</strong> To see if you are receiving unemployment benefits.</li><li><strong>NSFAS (National Student Financial Aid Scheme):</strong> To check for student stipends.</li><li><strong>Banks:</strong> To check for a monthly income above the set threshold (currently R620).</li></ul><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p><strong>The threshold:</strong> If any of these systems show a monthly income above R620, your application will be declined for that month.</p><h4 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="What_to_do">What to do</span></h4><ol start="1" class="wp-block-list"><li><strong>Check your status every month:</strong> The SASSA system performs a new check each month. Your status can change.</li><li><strong>Appeal the decision:</strong> If you believe the “Income Source Identified” status is an error, you must appeal. You can do this on the <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">official SASSA SRD appeal website</a>.</li><li><strong>Provide a valid reason:</strong> When you appeal, explain why the detected income source is incorrect (e.g., the money was a temporary deposit, or it’s an old, inactive account).</li><li><strong>Confirm your details:</strong> Ensure your personal and banking information is up-to-date and correct on the SASSA website. An outdated or incorrect phone number can cause issues.</li></ol><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_SRD_Grant_Eligibility">SASSA SRD Grant Eligibility&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></h2><p>To receive the R370 (previously R350) SRD grant, you must successfully complete the application process and meet the eligibility criteria set by SASSA.</p><p>Here are the key requirements:</p><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>South African citizen, permanent resident or refugee&nbsp;</li><li>Age 18 to 60 years old&nbsp;</li><li>Unemployed</li><li>Not receiving any other social grants</li><li>Monthly income below R370 (previously R350)&nbsp;</li><li>Not receiving support from other govt COVID-19 initiatives</li></ul><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Grant_Types">SASSA Grant Types</span></h2><p>You can check SASSA grants amount with recent increase effective from October 2025 from table given below.</p><div class='code-block class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R530</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R530</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R560</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R570</td></tr><tr><td><a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-srd-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="321">Covid-19 Social Relief of<br>Distress (SRD)</a></td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R350</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R370</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R370</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R370</td><td class="has-text-align-center" data-align="center">R370</td></tr></tbody></table><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">SASSA Grants Payment Amount 2026</figcaption></figure><p>South Africa offers various social grants administered by the South African Social Security Agency (SASSA) to support its citizens in need. These grants provide financial assistance to vulnerable groups including the elderly, persons with disabilities, children, and veterans. To qualify for these grants, applicants must be South African citizens, permanent residents, or refugees with formal refugee status.</p><p>There are 8 main types of SASSA grants available:</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="1_Social_Relief_of_Distress_SRD_Grant">1. Social Relief of Distress (SRD) Grant</span></h3><p>The SASSA SRD R370 grant provides temporary financial relief to individuals facing dire economic circumstances. It was introduced during the COVID-19 pandemic to aid those who lost jobs and income. The grant is R370 (previously R350) per month.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-srd-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="321">SRD R370 (previously R350) Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="2_Older_Persons_Grant">2. Older Person’s Grant</span></h3><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>The old age grant supports men and women over 60 years old with no other income source. Applicants cannot reside in a state institution and must pass a means test. The grant amount is either R2,320 or R2,340 per month, depending on the beneficiary’s age.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-old-persons-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="301">Older Person’s Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="3_Disability_Grant">3. Disability Grant</span></h3><p>The disability grant provides income support to people between 18-59 years old with a mental or physical disability preventing employment for over 6 months. A medical assessment confirms disability status. The monthly amount is up to R2,320 on a sliding scale.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-disability-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="333">Disability Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="4_War_Veterans_Grant">4. War Veteran’s Grant</span></h3><p>Veterans who fought in World War 2 or the Korean War and are over 60 years or disabled can apply for this grant. Recipients cannot live in a state institution or receive other grants, and must pass a means test. The monthly grant is R2,340.</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-war-veterans-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="468">War Veteran’s Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="5_Child_Support_Grant">5. Child Support Grant</span></h3><p>This grant assists parents/primary caregivers struggling to provide for children under 18 years. Applicants must be South African residents and the biological parent or primary caregiver. The grant is <strong>R570 per month</strong>, plus a <strong>R280 top-up</strong>, <strong>totaling R850</strong>.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-child-support-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="326">Child Support Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="6_Foster_Child_Grant">6. Foster Child Grant</span></h3><p>The foster child grant supports children formally placed in foster care by court order until age 18. The monthly grant of <strong>R1,260 per month</strong> is paid to the assigned foster parent to help cover costs.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-foster-child-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="329">Foster Child Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="7_Care_Dependency_Grant">7. Care Dependency Grant</span></h3><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>This grant is for caregivers of children under 18 years with severe permanent mental/physical disabilities requiring full-time care at home. Applicants must submit medical proof and cannot have the child in state institutional care. The grant amount is <strong>R2,320 per month</strong>.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-care-dependency-grant/" data-type="page" data-id="336">Care Dependency Grant</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h3 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="8_Grant-in-Aid">8. Grant-in-Aid</span></h3><p>This supplementary grant is for recipients of the Older Person’s, Disability, or War Veteran’s grant who require regular attendant care and assistance with daily activities. A means test and medical assessment are required. The Grant-in-Aid grant amount is <strong>R560 per month</strong>.</p><p>Check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/sassa-grant-in-aid/" data-type="page" data-id="339">Grant-In-Aid</a> article for more detail on this type of SASSA grant.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Status_Check_Service_Not_Available_Website_Down">SASSA Status Check Service Not Available: Website Down</span></h2><p>Sometimes the official SASSA Status Check website is down and it shows the error message,</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p><strong><em>“The Service is unavailable at the moment.<br>Please try again later.”</em></strong></p><p>as you can see in below screenshot.</p><div class="wp-block-image"><figure class="aligncenter size-large has-custom-border"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1024" height="541" src="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Website-Down-showing-The-Service-is-unavailable-at-the-moment-1024x541.webp" alt="SASSA Website Down showing The Service is unavailable at the moment" class="has-border-color has-theme-palette-2-border-color wp-image-578" style="border-width:2px" srcset="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Website-Down-showing-The-Service-is-unavailable-at-the-moment-1024x541.webp 1024w, https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Website-Down-showing-The-Service-is-unavailable-at-the-moment-300x159.webp 300w, https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Website-Down-showing-The-Service-is-unavailable-at-the-moment-768x406.webp 768w, https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/wp-content/uploads/2024/04/SASSA-Website-Down-showing-The-Service-is-unavailable-at-the-moment.webp 1200w" sizes="auto, (max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px"><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">SASSA Website Down: The Service is unavailable at the moment</figcaption></figure></div><p>In such cases, you can use our <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/">SRD Status Check</a> page to check your status within no time.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Contact_Details">SASSA Contact Details</span></h2><p>If you need to speak to a SASSA agent about your application or status, contact them through:</p><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><ul class="wp-block-list"><li>Toll-free call center: <a href="tel:+27800601011">0800 601 011</a></li><li>WhatsApp support: <a href="tel:+27820540016">082 054 0016</a></li><li>Email: <a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#ff988d9e918b9a918e8a968d969a8cbf8c9e8c8c9ed1989089d1859e"><span class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="1a7d687b746e7f746b6f7368737f695a697b69697b347d756c34607b">[email&#160;protected]</span></a>&nbsp;</li><li>Visit your nearest SASSA office – find locations on the website</li><li>Twitter: <a href="https://twitter.com/OfficialSASSA" target="_blank" rel="noopener">@OfficialSASSA</a></li><li>Facebook: <a href="https://www.facebook.com/SASSANewsZA" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA News</a></li></ul><p>Reach out via your preferred channel to get personalized assistance with any questions or issues related to your SASSA grant application.</p><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="FAQs_about_SASSA_Status_Check">FAQs about SASSA Status Check</span></h2><p>Check the following commonly asked questions and their answers about SASSA. These answers are provided according to the best of our knowledge, but you are suggested to confirm any specific data from official source as well.</p><div id="rank-math-faq" class="rank-math-block"><div class="rank-math-list "><div id="faq-question-1730925564909" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_check_SASSA_Status_Online">How to check SASSA Status Online?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>You can use our SASSA Status checking tool <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/#SASSA_Status_Check_Online">here</a>. You need to provide your South African ID Number and Phone Number to check your SASSA status for SRD R370 (previously R350) and other grants. Our SASSA Status checking tool fetch the official record and is blazingly fast as compared to the official SASSA website. In case, you find any issue with our tool you can use the SASSA tool <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/status" target="_blank" rel="noopener">here</a>.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730925985659" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_check_SASSA_Status_without_data">How to check SASSA Status without data?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>You can your SASSA SRD R370 status on your mobile phone by dialing <strong><a href="tel:*120*69277#">*120*3210#</a></strong> or <strong><a href="tel:*120*69277#">*120*69277#</a></strong>. You do not need an active internet connection or data to check your SASSA Status by this method.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730928217482" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_change_SASSA_phone_number">How to change SASSA phone number?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>You can change your SASSA phone from the <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/contact" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA contact portal</a> online. You can go to <em><strong>https://srd.sassa.gov.za/sc19/contact</strong></em> and enter your SASSA South African ID Number and Application ID. After that you will have to enter your new Phone Number and then receive an OTP on that Phone Number for verification. It may take about 24 hours to change your mobile phone number in the SASSA record. For more details you can check <a href="https://sassacheckstatus.co.za/changing-sassa-phone-number/">Changing SASSA Phone Number</a>.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730928488532" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_much_is_the_SASSA_Child_Support_Grant_in_2026">How much is the SASSA Child Support Grant in 2026?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>From October 2025, the SASSA Child Support Grant is R570 per month. There is also an additional Child Support Grant Top-Up of R850 available.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730929921634" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_much_is_the_SASSA_SRD_R370_Grant_in_2026">How much is the SASSA SRD R370 Grant in 2026?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>From October 2024, the SRD Grant amount is R370 per month which was previously R350. There is currently no increase in SRD grant amount from October 2025.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730930387404" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_change_SASSA_banking_details">How to change SASSA banking details?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>To change your SASSA banking details, access the <a href="https://services.sassa.gov.za" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA services website</a> at <strong><em>https://services.sassa.gov.za</em></strong> and select the “Bank Details Change” option. You’ll need to provide your ID number and specify your grant type. The process requires you to upload your ID copy, a recent bank confirmation letter or statement (not older than 3 months), and proof of residence. If you prefer in-person service, visit any SASSA office with your original ID and banking documents. A SASSA official will assist you in completing the bank details change form. The verification and updating process usually takes 3-5 working days.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730930543970" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_submit_SASSA_Appeal_if_grant_is_rejected">How to submit SASSA Appeal if grant is rejected?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><p>The SASSA appeal process begins at <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA Appeal portal</a> (<strong><em>https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal</em></strong>) where you can submit a reconsideration request. You have to enter South African ID Number and Phone Number, which was used while submitting the application, in the Appeal form. You must submit your appeal within 30 days of rejection by entering your ID number and selecting the relevant months for appeal. Supporting documents strengthening your case should be included with your submission.</p></div></div><div id="faq-question-1730930558841" class="rank-math-list-item"><h3 class="rank-math-question "><span id="How_to_check_SASSA_Appeal_status">How to check SASSA Appeal status?</span></h3><div class="rank-math-answer "><div class='code-block code-block-7' style='margin: 20px auto; text-align: center; display: block; clear: both;'><div class="lazy" parent-unit="Csrd_Incontent_Lazy"></div></div><p>To check your appeal status, you can use the <a href="https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal" target="_blank" rel="noopener">SASSA website</a> (<strong><em>https://srd.sassa.gov.za/appeals/appeal</em></strong>). The appeal process typically takes 60-90 days for resolution. SASSA will notify you of the outcome through your preferred communication method.</p></div></div></div></div><h2 class="wp-block-heading"><span id="SASSA_Status_Check_Last_Words">SASSA Status Check: Last Words</span></h2><p>Checking your SASSA status online is easy and does not require you to visit the SASSA office physically or wait in the long queues of SASSA helpline number. On this page, you can simply enter your South African ID Number (Number of your South Africa ID Card) and Phone Number to perform SASSA Status Check (SRD Status Check). You can check your SASSA Status for R370 by using this tool as well. We make the regular updates to this tool so that you can check your grant status easily.</p><div class="lwptoc lwptoc-autoWidth lwptoc-baseItems lwptoc-light lwptoc-notInherit" data-smooth-scroll="1" data-smooth-scroll-offset="24"><div class="lwptoc_i"><div class="lwptoc_header">
